###unitednetherlands####
UNL = {

 #Dutch
  #Monarchy
		
	dynamic_country_name = { #Dictatorship
		name = dyn_c_unitednetherlands_absolutist_monarchy
		adjective = UNL_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
					has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
					has_law = law_type:law_military_junta
					has_law = law_type:law_single_party_state
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = { #Vote
		name = dyn_c_unitednetherlands_monarchy
		adjective = UNL_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_technocracy
					has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
					has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
					has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
					has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
  #Republic
	
	dynamic_country_name = { #Dictatorship
		name = dyn_c_unitednetherlands_dictatorship

					has_law = law_type:law_single_party_state

		name = dyn_c_castille_absolutist_monarchy
		adjective = CAS_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
					has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
					has_law = law_type:law_military_junta
					has_law = law_type:law_single_party_state
				}

  #United States
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_PHI_subject_USA
		adjective = PHI_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 100

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				is_subject_of = c:USA
				NOT = {
					is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
					is_subject_type = subject_type_personal_union
				}
			}
		}
	}

		adjective = EGY_ADJ

		priority = 100

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				is_subject_of = c:TUR
				NOT = {
					is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
					is_subject_type = subject_type_personal_union
				}
			}
		}
	}

	dynamic_country_name = { #Dictatorship
		name = dyn_c_netherlands_absolutist_monarchy
		adjective = NET_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
					has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
					has_law = law_type:law_military_junta
					has_law = law_type:law_single_party_state
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = { #Vote
		name = dyn_c_netherlands_monarchy
		adjective = NET_ADJ

CHL = {

  #France

	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_CHL_subject_FRA
		adjective = CHL_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 100

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				is_subject_of = c:FRA
				NOT = {
					is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
					is_subject_type = subject_type_personal_union
				}
			}
		}
	}

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				is_subject_of = c:GBR
				NOT = {
					is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
					is_subject_type = subject_type_personal_union
				}
				is_subject_type = subject_type_chartered_company
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_indiacompany_subject_GBR
		adjective = BIC_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 600

			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				is_subject_of = c:GBR
				NOT = {
					is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
					is_subject_type = subject_type_personal_union
				}
				NOT = { is_subject_type = subject_type_chartered_company }
			}
		}
	}

  #Sweden
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_denmark_subject_SWE
		adjective = DEN_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 100

		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = { 
				is_subject_of = c:SWE
				NOT = {
					is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
					is_subject_type = subject_type_personal_union
				}
			}
		}
	}
